[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1730[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39malphaMultiplyMode == AVIF_ALPHA_MULTIPLY_MODE_UNMULTIPLY[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1731[0m[39m:        avifResult result = [0m[1;35mavifRGBImageUnpremultiplyAlpha[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrgb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1732[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult != AVIF_RESULT_OK[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1733[0m[39m:            return result;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1734[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1735[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1736[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1737[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Convert pixels to half floats [0m[1;39m([0m[39mF16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, if necessary.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1738[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrgb->isFloat[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1739[0m[39m:        return [0m[1;35mavifRGBImageToF16[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrgb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1740[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1741[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1742[0m[39m:    return AVIF_RESULT_OK;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1743[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1744[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1745[0m[39m:typedef struct[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1746[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1747[0m[39m:#if [0m[1;35mdefined[0m[1;39m([0m[39m_WIN32[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1748[0m[39m:    HANDLE thread;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1749[0m[39m:#else[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1750[0m[39m:    pthread_t thread;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:798[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m818[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m798[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height * image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m >= [0m[1;36m0x1000[0m[39m && total_spill[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m> [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height * image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m3.[0m[39m8f[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m799[0m[39m:                        int a, b;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m800[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m801[0m[39m:                            a = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m802[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39melse[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m803[0m[39m:                            a = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m804[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m805[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m806[0m[39m:                            b = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m807[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39melse[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m808[0m[39m:                            b = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m809[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m810[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m811[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m812[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m813[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m814[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m815[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m816[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m817[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m818[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m   [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Issue Analysis and Root Cause[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The AddressSanitizer report pinpoints a dynamic stack buffer overflow in the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mslow-path function avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreformat.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, arising when [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“dampening” neighbor spill values.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the dampening block [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m798[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m818[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code computes offsets a and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mb based solely on pixel parity [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma = ±[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, b = ±[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without any subsequent bounds [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking. When pixels lie at the right or bottom edges, a or b remains +[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, causing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindices like `i+a == width` or `j+b == height` and triggering out-of-bounds [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads/writes on the stack‐allocated 2D arrays `uspill_image` and `vspill_image`.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The core YUV‐to‐RGB conversion, the iterative “spill” accumulation, and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneighbor distribution logic must remain intact to preserve color‐spill correction [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectness.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only the dampening branch will be fortified with boundary checks; no other [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode paths or harness logic are altered.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Patch Strategy[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Replace the existing dampening offset logic with bounded neighbor indices:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After computing the tentative neighbor offsets [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma, b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, clamp them so that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`i + a` and `j + b` always remain within `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, width−[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, height−[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrespectively.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Introduce local variables `ni` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneighbor i[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `nj` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneighbor j[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcapture the clamped indices. If the computed neighbor index falls outside the valid[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrange, fall back to the original pixel coordinate [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi or j[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, effectively skipping [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat neighbor’s dampening contribution.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Example patch outline within reformat.c:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Original dampening code around line [0m[1;36m798[0m[39m:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int a, b;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m a = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m a = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m b = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m b = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Replace with:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Compute neighbor indices with bounds clamping[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int ni = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mni < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mni >= image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ni = i;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int nj = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mj + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mj - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnj < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mnj >= image->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          nj = j;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Then perform dampening updates using [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi, j[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mni, j[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi, nj[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mni, nj[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m    -= pSpillCb;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m    -= pSpillCr;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mni[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m   -= pSpillCb;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mni[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m   -= pSpillCr;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mnj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m   -= pSpillCb;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mnj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m   -= pSpillCr;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mni[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mnj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m  -= pSpillCb;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mni[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mnj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m  -= pSpillCr;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Rationale[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This approach preserves both pixel‐parity logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchoosing +[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m or −[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintent to dampen four neighbors.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - By clamping out-of-bounds neighbor indices to the center pixel, we skip [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39millegal memory accesses while still applying a reduced dampening effect at edges.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Minimal invasive change: only the dampening block is modified, leaving the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrest of avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow untouched.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains existing behavior on interior pixels; edge pixels still receive some[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdampening [0m[1;39m([0m[39mat least on in-bounds neighbors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevents stack overflows without requiring dynamic allocations or altering [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray sizes.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to fuzzing harness, external libraries, or test code—the fix is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocalized to the source and ensures all existing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mYuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to pass.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slightly altered dampening at image edges: in original code, edge‐neighbor [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffsets could wrap into red zones causing UB. Now, edge neighbors are effectively [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskipped, which is a reasonable trade-off versus undefined behavior.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Performance impact is negligible [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcouple of integer comparisons[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - To validate, re-run regression tests and fuzz harness; observe no new failures[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand confirm AddressSanitizer no longer reports dynamic‐stack‐buffer‐overflow.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References to Similar Patterns[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The initial spill distribution in avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m784[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muses nearly identical neighbor logic combined with bounds checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi+adjCol >= [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwidth[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m adjCol = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Our fix parallels this pattern, centralizing neighbor [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindex clamping and improving safety.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
